This is actually a solid station stop that can connect to several routes including the Van Nuys/Studio City Dash, several Los Angeles Metro Rapids and actually has a restroom facility (although often not in order). A lot of people without homes dwell nearby unfortunately they're just trying to get by and there are some low traffic streets and blocks around the area.

There is a ton of parking here and the lot is never full.... plenty of terminals to purchase a card or reload and taptogo.<//text>

<Review>Reason to ride the orange line in North Hollywood.

Metro is converting its entire fleet of buses to zero emission buses. This transition to electric buses will provide a cleaner, quieter fleet & significantly lower environmental impacts.

On July 22, Metro is installing new bus charging station at the Orange line North Hollywood west parking lot through October 31, 2019. The parking lot is temporarily closed during this time. For alternative parking, please use the north, south or east parking lots at North Hollywood Station that are accessible from Chandler Boulevard or Cumpston Street.

About 30,000 people each day use the Orange Line, which connects commuters in Chatsworth & Woodland Hills with the Red Line subway‚Äôs northern terminus in North Hollywood.

Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority staffers wrote in a new report that, based on two days of checks along the transit line, about 25.9% of passengers either did not have a valid fare or had not paid correctly before boarding. Officials called the discovery frustrating & unexpected.

Passengers boarding Orange Line buses are supposed to touch their plastic TAP cards to a waist-height pillar that automatically deducts the fare from a pre-paid account. The platforms have no turnstiles to prevent passengers from boarding without paying, and the buses do not have fare boxes.< /Review><pics>None< /pics>< resp>

We recent switched vets from Paradise Vet Hospital down the street to Center Vet Clinic because we adopted a new dog from the pound and they offered a free exam for new pets.

I'm so glad we switched. As a multi-pet house with both a cat and a dog, I was pleased to see that they give each pet a separate waiting area as to avoid stress.

3<//rate>
< Text>
Descent local coffee house that serves rather basic fare.
Nothing special in terms of food, since they really do not have a proper full kitchen.  They mostly have items such as muffins & bagels.
If you want a full breakfast with lots of attention, some of the hotels down the road are better choices. Service is what you would expect from a coffee shop. There is no view & it is not especially comfy inside. It feels cramped when crowded.  While it can be a challenge to get a decent breakfast or a cup of coffee in Shell Beach, this is a solid choice
for coffee.  The nearest Starbucks is a few exits away on the 101, so if you just want a cup of Joe, this is it.<//Text>

My first choice go to dispensary in EDC. Wide variety of great quality buds, continually changing menu but hardly ever (once temporarily out of GDP this summer-wasn't hard to find a stand in) out of the backbone standards.
